I know that the usual territories are still counting on a legislative basis. This has to change. Europe should become one legislative territory. The old structures are just too small in times of fast digital transmission. Also the consumer does not understand what is happening when content is available here but not there. Lets use our new device called EUROPE for creating one good rule for all.

I'm a Copyright Holder, but often I'm a suer, when I have to create covers and/or arrangements. Right societies like SABAM/SACEM/GEMA/BMI/SIAE etc they are NOT transparent, despitethe EU norms! If you want to consult their database, about Rights, it almost impossible. I deposited many piece of music. But in the database you can see only the one generated rights. All the other ones are hidden and taken into a so called "ghost database", which is totally AGAINST ANY transparency Act! Thus even the final user, if she wants to know more about inhedited or else, has difficulties to do it.
